## ü™Ñ [CP-Ansible Playground](https://github.com/vdesabou/kafka-docker-playground/tree/master/other/cp-ansible-playground)

&nbsp;  [![CP 5.5.13](https://img.shields.io/badge/skipped-CP%205.5.13-lightgrey)](https://github.com/vdesabou/kafka-docker-playground/actions/runs/3795785677/jobs/6455301139) [![issue 3146](https://img.shields.io/badge/1/8-CP%206.0.11-red)](https://github.com/vdesabou/kafka-docker-playground/issues/3146) [![issue 3146](https://img.shields.io/badge/1/8-CP%206.1.9-red)](https://github.com/vdesabou/kafka-docker-playground/issues/3146) [![issue 3146](https://img.shields.io/badge/1/8-CP%206.2.8-red)](https://github.com/vdesabou/kafka-docker-playground/issues/3146) [![issue 3146](https://img.shields.io/badge/1/8-CP%207.0.7-red)](https://github.com/vdesabou/kafka-docker-playground/issues/3146) [![issue 3146](https://img.shields.io/badge/1/8-CP%207.1.5-red)](https://github.com/vdesabou/kafka-docker-playground/issues/3146) [![issue 3146](https://img.shields.io/badge/1/8-CP%207.2.3-red)](https://github.com/vdesabou/kafka-docker-playground/issues/3146) [![issue 3146](https://img.shields.io/badge/1/8-CP%207.3.1-red)](https://github.com/vdesabou/kafka-docker-playground/issues/3146) 

Easily play with Confluent Platform Ansible playbooks by using Ubuntu based Docker images generated daily from this [cp-ansible-playground](https://github.com/vdesabou/cp-ansible-playground) repository

There is also a Confluent Cloud version available [here](https://github.com/vdesabou/kafka-docker-playground/tree/master/ccloud/cp-ansible-playground/)
